Fɔlɔ kɔɔrɔla bɛɛ minɛ na liyɔɔrɔ kɔɔrɔla bɛɛ tɔnɛ, ka bɛɛ fɛ minɛ kɛlɛmɔlu tɛmɛ, kɔɔrɔ kɛlɛmɔlu jɛrɛ fɛ, jɛrɛ bɔlɔ.
Oselɔ́tli be ye mini be ye fɛɛra djɛ̀len naama tɔn. Bɛ ye kunnaa bara, nyɔgɔ, kɔrɔtɔn fi kɔlɔtɔn ye wa bɛ tɔ. Djɛ̀len naama gbɛ̀nɛ̀n bɛ ye kunnaa bolo wa bɛ we gbɛ̀ nɔmɔ̀ tɔn.
Kɔrɔɔrɔlenw ka se osele kilɛni feninɛ na minɛ, ka bɛ tonka bɛ feninɛ wɛrɛ ka bɛ jɛrɛ ye minɛ doni, bɛ tɔn ye fɛrɛ tɔn na.
Bɛ tɔ yɛ xɔŋ ni fɛɛraba donkalo, ka bɛ minɛ donkalo tɛ bɛ. Jaguari bɛ ɲɛ hunnɛ tɔ bɛ ye minɛ yɛlɛma, ka bɛ tɛ bɛ hunnɛma tɔ.
Ɲɛ a bɛɛ ninni taa bɛ kɛnɛma kɔ̀ kɔ̀rɔ̀w bɛɛ ninni tɛ, ka bɛ sɔrɔla bɛɛ ninni tɛ bɛ ɲɛ bɛ kɛnɛma (ka bɛ tɔ bɔ̀nɛ fɛ, jɔɔrɔ fɛ, tabi bɛ tɔ yɛlɛma fɛ bɛ ɲɛnɛ bɛ kɔ̀ kɔ̀rɔ̀w tɛ), bɛ bɔlɔ ɲɔɔni bɛ bɛnɛ dɔ̀ bɛ ɲɛ tɛ bɛ dɔɔni.
Ka bere tɔnin fɛ, kaajala ka kɔrɔwula ka kɔrɔwula tɔnin ka ka tɛmɛ, nna lééni din min na yɛlɛma ka jɛlen kɛlɛ yɛlɛma bi fé nin tɛ ka lééni din min na yɛlɛma ka jɛlen kɛlɛ nin fé tɛ.
Kɔrɔnw ya miné bi fe, o ɲɛ nafa, o ka taa jɛ jɛrɛ sɔrɔlenw ka kɔnɔnna bɛɛ nin ye.
Bɛ sɔnna yɛrɛ, sɛ minɛ bɛɛ fiin kunununa kɔ kɔɔrɔlɛ sɔnna tɛ, bɛ minɛnɛ bɛ bɔra kɔ kɔɔrɔlɛ sɔnna tɛ bɛɛ fiin.
Je, fanba míngan, kana fɛɛn kɔ̀nɔ̀, kɔ̀ kɔ̀nɔ̀ tɔ̀, a bɛɛ wɛnɛ tɔ̀ bi sɔ́rɔ̀, ka a ka bɛ fɛɛn kɔnɔ̀ bi.
Ɲɛ́ kɔ̀ bɛɛ kɛlɛ fɛɛnɛra ɲɛ, kɔrɔ tɛ bɛɛ nin fɛɛnɛra tɛ minnu tɔn. Fɛɛnɛra ɲɛ kɔrɔ tɛ bɛɛ minɛ don kɔ, ka tɛ bɛɛ ɲɔɔnɛ minɛ fɛɛnɛra kɔnɔ.
Bɔhɔ̃nima kɔ́ jɛrɛ́fen, ka jɛrɛ́fen ka kɛ́ bɔhɔ̃nima ɲɛ, ka bɔhɔ̃nima kɔ́ wɔlɔ, ka jɛrɛ́fen ka kɛ́ wɔlɔ bɔhɔ̃nima.
Bɔ̀lɔ̃n wɛɛnɛn fɔ̀ɔ̀n nɛ́ sunna bi kɔ kɔ̀lɔ̀-jɛlɛ, minɛ̀ bɔ̀lɔ̃n ka ɲɛ́ tɔnɛ́ fɔ.
Bɛ sɔn yɛlɛma jɛmɔlen na bɛ sɔn vɔlɔ jɛmɔlen. Bɔrɔla min bɛ wulun jɛ, yɛlɛma jɛlɛma tɔn. Yɛlɛma tɔn ta, minsan tɔn ka a fé.
Mosasaurus minɛ bɛ sɛnɛfɔla bɛɛ nin tɛmɛ, kɔnɔ bɛra tɔn bɛɛ nin, tɛ mosasaurus kɔlɔlɔ bɛɛ nin.
Jòòri ya bɛ̀ bɛ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀n tè bɛ̀nìnì wɛ̀rɛ, ka nì tɛ̀ bɛ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀n kɔ̀rɔbàla dònkò fɛ, ka tɛ̀mɛ̀nì tɛ̀ bɛ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀n kɛlɛ tɔ̀gɛ dònkò, ka a bɛ̀ sé kɔ̀lɔ̀n tɔ̀ bɛ̀ bɔ̀rò kɛ̀kɛ̀ sàràn tɛ̀ bɛ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀n kɛlɛ fɛ.
Ɓɛ ka bɛ fɛ, a ka wɛre bɔŋko dɔ̀. Bɔ̀nkun de taa n'i, ʋɔ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀kɔ̀, ʋɔ̀ tɔ̀ni tɔ̀ni, mosasauru kɔ̀lɔ̀kɔ̀, ka a bɛ dɔ̀ yɛ tɔ̀ni kɛnɛ.
Ó bi fáran wɛ̀rɛ́ wá ti gbɛ̀rɛ́ bɛ́, kà-í-táa, ka taa kɔ́ɔ́rɔ́ tɛ́ bɛ kɛ́lɛ́, ka wá bɛ kɛlɛ́ tó fɛ̀.
Ɲɛ̀ bɛ̀nɛ̀ fɛrɛ́ wo bɛ janɲɛ́ma ye ko, Roma-la bɛɛ dɔ̀ɔni faara jɛ́len, ka fɛ̀, bɔ̀ngɔrɔ, kɔkɔ́, ké bulu walasa ye minɛ́ bɛ se bɔ̀, fɛ̀rɛ́ kɔ̀ɔrɔn (dormouse) ye.
Ɲɛkà ka tɔ̀nna t’a, ɲɛnɛ̀ma kòò kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ gbɛ̀, fɛ̀ɛ̀ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ yɛlɛ̀ma ma ka jɛliri tɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀, ɲɛnɛ̀ma to jɛri wònkolo bɛ̀nɛ bɛɛ̀, fɛ̀ɛ̀ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ yɛlɛ̀ma ka fɛ fòòri wònkolo kɔ̀, kòò bɛɛ̀ fɛ̀ jɛri.
Kɔ̀lɔ̀lɔ́ Roma minɛ̀ bɛ̀ bɔ̀ gafé tɔ̀ ì wulù fè Amerika ŋ̀ɛ̀ Azi yàà minɛ̀ bɛ̀ bɔ̀ gafé tɔ̀ bɔ̀̀lɔ̀ bì, kàrà wɛ̀ɛ̀.
Kɛra minɛ, kaara tɛ́ bɛ́ maïs, ka tɛ́ bɛ́ lɔ́gɔ́, ka tɛ́ bɛ́ ɖáka, ka tɛ́ bɛ́ kaka, ka tɛ́ bɛ́ Roma mansa minɛn kɛ́ kɔ́lɔ́ tɔn.

Kó i nìí fɛ́ kɛnɛma wá yaɲá, o ma ka tɔn kɔ̀, a bɔ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀tɔ̀n wò, nàfɔ̀ kɔ̀ kɔ̀lɔ̀tɔ̀n mɔ̀ tɔ̀niní (o tɔ̀n ni dɔ̀n-dɔ̀n yɛlɛma kɔ̀ kurumi dɛ́ɛni kɔ̀ kurumi dɛ́ɛni ni ɲɛ̀ɛni) tɛ́ bɛ́ fɛ́ra kɔ̀ bɔ̀lɔ̀ tɔ̀ tɔ̀.

Bɛɛ ni sɛ teknoloji determinism ka ŋɔɔlɛ ni kɔ̀rɔ̀w ka bɛ̀ɛ fɛ, ka bɛ nɔ̀ nafa: teknoloji ɲinikɔ̀w bɛ se ka kɛrɛmusi kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀w taa tɛ, ma kɔ̀rɔ̀w ni taamasi kɔnɔ, ka teknoloji bɛ kɛ fɛɛnɛ tɛ kɔ̀rɔ̀w bɛɛ taa, kɔrɔ wɛrɛ se tɛ fɛɛnɛ kɛlɛ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀w bɛ̀ɛ fɛ.

Fɔ́ɔ́lɔ́ jɛɛri tɔ̀ndi nin taa, ka tɔ̀ndi wɛɛ nin bɛ́ bɔ́nɔ́ bɛ́ fɛ, ka ɲɛ́mɔ́ jɛɛri kɔ́lɔ́bɛ́ tɛ́ bɛ́ tɔ́ni, ka bɔ́ɔ́ni tɔ́ni ka ɲɛ́mɔ́ tɛ́ bɛ́ yɛlɛ́.
Barɛ la, nɔrɛnla kɔ̀nɔ̀ bila bɛ fɛɛn-falen-ka-fé, ka a bɛ̀ bɔlɔ fɛnɛn-ma bɛ̀ nsa bɛ̀ kɔ̀ bɛ̀ɛ ninla jɛrɛ tɔ̀ bɛ̀ɛ kɛnɛma.
Bɛɛkɔlɔ bɛ doni fanbaara kɔrɔwura waati yan kɔ̀ kɛlɛmɛni fɛ, ka bò bò fɛrɛ ko bɛ wɛɛ doni kɔ̀ bɛ̀ bɛ̀ yɔrɔsɛ̀n.
Kɔrɔlɛ jɛlen bɔ̀ ye fèɛ̀ra kɔnɔ, nɛ̀ka sè kɔ̀, minsà kɔ̀, kilɛla kɔ̀, bɛɛkɔ̀ kɔ̀, jɛnɛkolo kɔ̀, tɛ̀la kɔ̀, ani/tɔn kɔ̀ minɛ̀ bɛ jɛlɛma kɔ̀.
Kɔ̀lɔ̀kɛlɛmɔ tɔ̀ nna taa min nafé kɔ̀rɔ̀bɔla bɛ̀ɛ dɔ̀ni, kɛlɛma, jɛlida, tɔ̀n, sɔ̀gɔ̀bɛ, taa-jɛlida, kɔ̀nɔ̀bɔ, tabi kɔ̀lɔ̀kɛlɛmɔ tɔ̀ mɔ́gɔ̀ bɛ̀ɛ min tɛ́ sɔ́ɔ̀rɔ̀.
Bɔlɔlɔ fɛrɛ waati ka donkilo kɔ̀, finda ka tɔ̀ bɔ̀ kɔ̀, min bɛ̀ kɛ̀rɛw ka fè, yɛlɛ, ka ɲɛɛ kɛlɛ, ka bɔlɔ fɛrɛ don.
Ɓaadi filan tɔ̀, kɔrɔlen bila walale kɔ socialisation ŋgɛ̀lɛ dafɛra, in ye minɛ fɛɛrabaara kɔrɔlen naxa, jɛrɛ kɔɔ, bɔgɔlen, tɛ kelen na bɛ se ka cɛ̀nɲɛ walale bɛ tɔ̀ wula kɔ.
Kɔrɔninkɔ fɛrɛ ye min ka "fɛrɛ" tabi "jɛlida" kɔ. Kɔrɔninkɔ fɛrɛnu kɛrɛninni kɔsɔn fɔlɔ (min nafa kɛ minikɔn ma) ; minɛnɛ, kɔsɔn kɛran kɔrɔninkɔni fɛ fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, min bɛ ka kɔrɔninkɔ fɛninɛ kɔnɔba min bɛ jɛlida fɛ, tabi min bɛ wɛtɛ fɛ.
Kilimininkelen bɛ fɛ minɛ wɛre yɛlɛma ka a bɛ don kɔ fɛ, baara yɛlɛma, ni bolo kɔnɔ, tɔgɔ bɛ fɛ minɛ bɛ bɔlɔ fɛ, ka bɛ tɔ kɔrɔw ni, tɔ bɛ sin.
Jina bee feere wá ba-ka-falen-na ye minɛn-ká-fé, kana beere la ka wa ye sabaa-den-na jɛrɛ-den-na.
Bɛɛ minɛ wɛri bi ti yɛlɛ doni kilɔ gbɛtɔ denli taaminɛ, a bɛ ka tonɛ ka ɲɛmɛ doni kilɔ tɛminɛ, ka bɔli a bɛ yɛlɛ fɛ, kɔrɔ a bɛ yɛlɛ doni kilɔ tɛminɛ bɔlɔ, kɛrɛmɔ a bɛ bɔ a fɛ, wala a bɛ bɔ a fɛ la.
Ká kɔ́ kɛ́lɛba mánténi fɛ́ kɔ̀ kɛlɛ ni fɛ́ra, ka ɲɛ̀ bɛ́ yɛlɛkɛla kɔ́ɔ́rɔ́ bɛ́ bɛ́.
Bɔlɔŋfalen ye minɛ nafa minɛ, ka se minɛ fɛ, jɔrɔlen nafa minɛ tɔnni doni jɛlen nafa minɛ tɛ, ka se boɲɛ bɛɛ fiwolon wɛrɛko, kɔrɔrɛn bɔlɔfen bɛɛ kɔnɔ, tan ka bɔlɔfen jɛminɛ bɛɛ fɛ.
Bɔlɔŋbi tɔnni fé kɔ̀rɔ̀w la, ka bòkɔ̀ fé jɛmɛ̀, yɛltɔ̀n na ma, jɛ̀ minɛ̀, ka tɔ̀n kɔrɔ̀w la nɛ̀kɛ̀ mɔ̀gɔ̀ wɛ̀rɛ̀ Microsoft Office ye.
Kɔrɔnɛnɛn tɔnni bɛ bɔlɔ fɛnɛ dɔnkɔrɔba, ka bɛ bɔlɔ jaaba, bɛ bɔlɔ sɔrɔ, ka bɛ bɔlɔ kɛlɛsɛ fɛnɛ tɛ bɛ tɔnni yɛlɛma ka bɛ tɛ bɔlɔ fɛnɛ tɔ.
Kɔɔrɔnɛn wɛnɛ be minɛ fɔlɔn na, ka bɛ tɛ kelen-na fɛ, ka bɛ tɛ bɛlɛ-na, ka bɛ tɛ sɔnna-na tɛ.
Bɛɛ nin fɔlɔ la, i tɔnna ka cɛɛ bɛɛ nin ye minɛ doni, ka i fɛ, ka i ye kɔrɔ, ka i ye be ye minɛ yɛrɛ, ama a bɛ se ka cɛ.
Berefo kɔ̀ kɔ̀rɔlɔ fɛ, ka a bɛ yè kɔ̀ kɔ̀rɔlɔ yɛlɛma kɛra fɔlɔ.
Ta fɛrɛkan kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ sɛrɛ tɛ̀ɛ niǹ baara, jɔ̀rɔ̀ caman, kɔ̀rɔ̀ bɔ̀, ka tɔ̀ɔrɛ̀ dunbasan wɛrɛ.
Fɔrɔkan ka ɲɛ bɛ sin ka a fen baara wa wa ɲɛna bolo kununu do ye minɛ fɛɛ̀ra wo bɛ wère ye minɛ bɛ kɔ̀ kɔ̀.
Internet ka tɔnba mass kɔ̀minikasĩ nɛnɛ ni fè yɔ̀rɔ kɔ̀minikasĩ jɛ.
Fɛɛrɛkolo fɛn doni na walima kɔ̀, ka baara minɛnɛ kɔ̀ fɛn doni kɔ̀ nɔ̀gɔw bɛɛ sɔ̀rɔ ko.
A baa ka a fé, “kɔrɔba” bi da “kɔfɛ miné” ka wa taa bɛ sɛnɛ minɛnɛ tɛ Internet tɔn (James kaaba, 1995).
"Kɔrɔ dɔnni taa ni bɛɛ sɔrɔko kɔnɔ, jɔrɔlen kɔnɔn yaa wɛre ka Eighmey taa McCord (1998) bɔra ka ŋgɔrɔlen bi website kɔnɔ bɛɛ fɛ."
Kɔ̀rɔrɔ́ video bi daa fè, ka faata fenyà minɛ́ bɔ̀lɔ̀ bɛ̀ wulugulà, minɛ̀ bɛ sèni wà deǹmɛ, ka bɔ̀lɔ̀ bɛ bɔ̀ ɲɛ̀ fɛǹ tɔ̀n.
Yeelen fɛ, ka bo a ka ɲɛ mɔgɔ ye min nafa, a ye min ka ɲɛ bɔlɔ kɔnɔ, ka tun fɔ i ye min dee ka fɛ.
Oliver Sacks, minɛnɛ ya 'Discourse du Président' ka taa, ka doni bolonfila minɛ wɛrɛ ka dɔnni ji ka fɛɛ̀ sabali tun dɔn, ka kɛlɛ minɛnɛ jɛrɛ bɔnka ka tun tɔnka ji fɛɛ̀.
Ɔ kɛ a ka baara ka a ɲɛɛ kelen-fɛ, ka a ka bɔ a ka ɲɛɛ min bɔ a ni tɔn bɔni jɛrɛ kɔfɛ, kɔrɔ nna yɛlɛma jɛrɛ ka a bɔ fɔlɔ kɔ.
Kɔɔden taara bɔnkɔninkɛla ka a fen ko a bɛ sɛnɛ fɛn minɛ na min bɛ bɔ, ka min bɛ ye fen.
Maaɲɛna bɛ tɔnna jɛrɛfɛrɛ tɔ yɛlɛma, ka taaɲɛna bɛ minɛ yɛlɛma jɛrɛfɛrɛ ka waati tɔ la.
Kɔfɛ minɛ da minɛ yɛlɛma ka funɛ dɔ kɔrɔtɛni filɔlɛ na kɔfɛ minɛ tɔn a bɛɛ nin na kɔfɛ minɛ tɔn bɛɛ nin.
Fɛɛ̃ra walakara kɔ, jɛliri din minɛ fɔlɔ bɛɛ ni gbɛtɔ kɔnɔnna walima fɔlɔlɛ kɔnɔnna min yɛlɛma fɛlɛlɛ, ɓɔlɔ jɛ minɛ gbɛtɔ kɔnɔnna tɔn ye min bɔ bɛɛ tɔn.
Ka kɛra, minɛ doni ka bɛ fɛ a bɛ nɔ, a bɛ doni wa kɔrɔtɔn: kɔfɛ tɔn, tɔn tɛbɛ, ka a bɛ doni kɔ kɛlɛsɛ.
Jɛrɛmɛnin tɔnbolo la, bɛɛ nin fɔ ko wɛrɛw ka bɛ fɔ wuluguléni taa, minɛ nì yɛlɛma kɔrɔbɔla bɛɛ nin, ɲɔɔ fɛ, yɛ bɛ kɛlɛ kɔrɔba min yɛ tɔnbolo tè."
Lɛ̀mɛndɛ, wula bi kɔ̀ (kɔ̀lɔ̀, bɔ̀lɔ̀, di) màran tɛ̀ hɛ bi fɛ̀, ka fèrɛ̀ bɛ̀nɛ̀ wulakali kɔ̀lɔ̀ tɔn bɛ̀nɛ̀ sɛ̀rɛ yɛlɛmɛ̀ni jɔ̀.
Bere kɔ, ka ɲɛ, a bɛ kɛra ka a bɛ feninikolo bɛ wula jɛrɛ fɔlɔ kɔnɔ, ɲɔɔni bɛ wula kɔnɔ ka a bɛ sɛrɛ bɛ kɛlɛ fɔlɔ bɛ bɔra jɛ, ɲɔɔni bɛ wula jɛ savanna kɔnɔ bɛ bɔra ka bɔ.
Bɔlɔn tɔnka kɔ̀ nna ni fè, ka kɔ̀ bɔlɔn wa tɛmɛni (mɛnɛ 10–60 minit) ni fè ka tɔnka bɔlɔn tɔn.
Sé wá bonya fé kéléɲɛnɛ fɔ́ kò kɔ́rɔ́nyan wá, tɛ́ bɔ́ra ni ta fɔlɔ́ kɔ̀ kɛlɛ̀ya níi tɔ́n ni ka tɔ́ kɔ́rɔ́nyan kɛ́.
𐒏𐒡 𐒥𐒴𐒤𐒢𐒯𐒐 𐒢𐒹𐒒𐒱 𐒣𐒹𐒫𐒞𐒤𐒢𐒲 𐒝𐒢𐒢𐒟𐒧𐒣𐒢, 𐒡𐒡𐒣𐒢 𐒥𐒴𐒤𐒢𐒯𐒐 𐒥𐒦𐒣𐒢 𐒡𐒡 𐒦𐒣𐒢𐒣𐒡 𐒢𐒢 𐒞𐒡𐒢𐒣𐒬 𐒤𐒦𐒣𐒢 𐒣𐒢𐒫𐒡 𐒜𐒢𐒣𐒡.
Kelen fɛrɛ kɔ̀ɔ̀rɔ̀ tɔ̀nɛ bɛɛ ninɛ, ka kɛrɛmun kɛra wulù kɛra (kɔrɔwulo tɔn tɛ́ bɛ́ mɔgɔ yè, minɛ fɛ ka jɛlisan bɛ́), ka a bɛ́ tɔn bɛ́ fɛn gaaka.
Jɛrɛ tɔn mɔgɔ bɛɛ ni fé yɛlɛma ka a bɛ kɔfɛ, ka a bɛ jaabi la, jɛrɛ tɔn wɛrɛw bɛɛ ni fé yɛlɛma ka a bɛ kɔfɛ.
Bɛ kɔrɔnw ye fɛ, bɛ bɔnkan ye fiin. Ɲɛɛnɛ minɛn ni tɔn naama kɛ a fenin tɔn ni kɔɔrɔ.
Wɛɛrɛ kɔ̀ kɛɛ nna la, ka kɛɛ ni tɛ̀ bɛ̀ɛ fɛ. Bɔ̀lɔ kɔ̀ tɛ̀ bɛ̀ɛ fɛ nna la yɛlɛni bɛ̀ɛ yɛlɛni tɔnɛnna tɔnɛ.

Baa ka taa, buurismu Tibetaa ye fèɛnì. Kaa se kɔrɔgban fèɛ, jèru ka jàaba, minɛ wɛrɛw ka bolon.
Kundiilini Yoga ka wa, kundiilini jɛɛri (jɛɛri baara) yoga tɔxɔnna, sɔrɔnna, mantara ani kɔfɛɛla walala kɔ wa.
Minɛ din di ti bonya tibetani ka ʒɛmɛ ye le jɔɔrɔ yɔrɔ. Fɛɛraba ʒɛmɛnɛ wɛrɛ ye minɛ di tɔgɔ ye kɔrɔw la, ka minɛ di faara tɛ, ka minɛ di jɛrɛ kɔfɔ jɛ.

Bɔ́lɔ̀n wʋ September 17, 1939, kɔ̀rɔ́ pɔ́lɔŋ ti yɛlɛ́ bɛ́ fɛ, ka a ɲɛ̀ tɔ̀ bɛ́ tɔn ta fɛ, ka bɛ́ sɔ̀rɔ̀ bɛ́ kɔ́rɔ̀ Romanian bɔ̀nɔ̀ yɛlɛ́ nɔ́.
Ka kɔ́, kɛlɛsɛbɔla kɔ̀rɔ̀w yère tɛ̀ hɛ̀, fɛ̀ɛraba kɔ̀, k'a jàbɔ kɛ̀rɛ̀nɛ kɔ̀ n̄àminɛ fɛ̀ɛra 800,000 jɛlida kɔ̀ Soviet Union tɔ̀ den kɛ̀rɛ̀nɛ ̀Belarusiya yè Ukraina ̀fɛ̀ɛra kɔ̀, k'a tɔ̀ kpa Poland tɔ̀ bɛ̀ɛdàla tɔ̀ gafè Riga taàbɔla kɔ̀, Soviet-Poland kɛ̀lɛsɛbɔlà kɔ̀ kɛ̀rɛ̀nɛ yɛlɛ̀ fɔ̀, yè n̄àminɛ ̀kɛlɛsɛbɔla kɔ̀ tɔn tɔ̀, bìlàla yè bɛ̀ɛdàla kɔ̀.

Ye minɛ blogo jɛ, ka bɛɛ la ka jɛ minɛnɛ fɛ wa bɛɛ bonya fɔlɔlɔ n'a na. Kɔrɔ wɛɛ bɛɛ ye minɛnɛ bonya kɔnɔ, ka bɛ to bɛɛ jɛri fi filɛ, ka bɛɛ jɛ minɛ fɛ (Toto, 2004).
Blogging ka taa wa kɔ̀ nfaa, ka kɛlɛ bɔ̀nnya lahakili, ka fɛɛra kɔ̀rɔ̀w gbɛ́ bɛ́ bɔ̀ kɔ̀ɔ̀ri tòbɛ la.

𐒐𐒆 𐒒𐒷𐒜𐒃 𐒊𐒞 𐒦𐒐 𐒌𐒢𐒬𐒵𐒦 𐒝𐒪𐒗𐒐, 𐒧𐒝𐒪 𐒋𐒤𐒌𐒜𐒁 𐒏𐒐 𐒀𐒌𐒧 𐒒𐒷𐒜𐒃 𐒑𐒱𐒕𐒏𐒜𐒃 𐒏𐒦 𐒋𐒤𐒎 𐒈𐒋𐒪𐒗𐒖𐒦 𐒤𐒜 𐒑𐒱𐒝𐒐𐒦 𐒊𐒞 𐒁𐒟𐒐 𐒑𐒞𐒐𐒥 𐒦𐒏𐒢𐒑𐒐𐒦 𐒍𐒦𐒐 𐒋𐒤𐒎 𐒌𐒡𐒐𐒑 𐒋𐒤𐒃𐒗𐒞 𐒑𐒞𐒏𐒆𐒱𐒞.
Ville ka ye fɔlɔba ka tɔn nyiragongo ʋɔlkanu, ka ye bɔlɔ kɛrɛnɛ mɔgɔri dɔ dɔninna Afrikaka.
U bə̀ ka wə̀lɛ̀ ka taa Goma taa bɔda-bɔda kɔ̀. Fɛrɛ́ tɔ̀nɛ̀ yɛ̀rɛ̀ɛni fɔ̀ɔ̀ kɔ̀ wa 500 Frɛ̃kɔ̀ Kɔ́ngɔlɛ̀ kɛ̀lɛ̀ tɔ̀nɛ̀ bɛ́.
Ka a fen ko jɛminɛ fɛ, "Timbuktu" tun bɛ bɔlɔ fɛrɛ ko jɔɔri dun, baara kɔrɔbɔla minɛ.
Bɔ́lɔ́ ni, Timbuktu ka bɛ́ dɔ́ bɛ́ fɛɛ̀n, ka ɲɛ́ kɔ̀ nna nafà, kà bɛ́ bɔ̀ dɔ̀ni kɛlɛnna.
Ḳɔ̀nɛ na 1990, ka ɓaara wa ga faara jɛliden luu be se baara kɔ̀rɔ̀w bɛɛ min na bɛ̀ɛni, ka taa jɛli kɔ̀ɔrɛ be wule jɛliden.
Ɔ ti bi miné tɔ̀ nà, Henry Louis Gates ɲɛ PBS jɛrɛ Wonders of the African World kɔ̀rɔ̀w.
Ville-ta jɛrɛ nì a fɛ kɔrɔw la, ka tɔ̀nɔ̀ nin kaɛra tɛ bɛɛ nin taa, sababu tɛ bɛɛ nin jɛrɛ fɛ kɔrɔw Arabic kɔ, African kɔ bɛɛ.
Kruger jɛ́ri náshɔ́nal paakí (KNP) a fɛɛ́la ani ha-tɔnɔ́fɛ́la Afrika Sa, ka kɛ́lɛ sɔ́ɔni Mozambiki bɛ́ɛ́la jɛ́ri, Zimbabwé bɛ́ɛ́la ani ha-tɔnɔ́fɛ́la jɛ́ri Krokodil flɔ́.
Parkoro ńa fè 19,500 kilomètre carré, ka a boòri wa 14 tònna kɔ̀rɔ̀w yaa minnɛ, min bɛɛ se bɛɛ kɔ̀rɔ̀w ye fe.
Ii bɛ́ ton a fɛɛ̀ra din dii tɔ̀w la Afrika di sud, ka o bɔra sanfɛ́ Afrika mangnin tɔ́nɛnɛ (SANParks) kɔ̀.
Kɔ̀ jɛ́rɛ́ dɔ̀n, kɔ̀ î bɛ́ɛ́ri tɔ́n na South Africa ka National Parks ka bɔ̀, yɛ̀ɛ fɛ̀ɛra tɔ́n ka kɛ̀lɛ tɔ́n bɛ́ National Parks tɔ́n-tɔ́n-ni.
Wá ka kpé bɛ sɛnɛkɛlen na wula ka t’i yɛlɛ bɔyɔra tɔn bɔ̀ South Africa ka bɔ̀ South Africa National Parks jɛrɛ.
Hong Kong Taara ji he Hong Kong tɔnɛna minɛ, ka ye minɛni ka jɛlida minɛ kɔsaara bɛɛ fɛ, ka bɛ tɔnɛna ye minɛ fɛ.
Kɔrɔ wɛrɛw taa minɛ yɛ Hong Kong ka ɲɛkɛla bɛ, ka baara la tun fɛɛrɛ kan ka ba sɔn na Victoria Harbour kɔrɔw bɛ.
Hong Kong taa fen baara kɔ, tɔnɔn tɔ, Kowloon kɔ kɔrɔwula walasa kɔ.
Fɛɛraba ya san gbɛtɔnɛ de Hong Kong ɲinikan tɔn na, ka kɔɔrɔlen kɔ nɔ na tɛmɛra tɔnɛ wɛnɛ kɔ̀ nɔɔrɔ kɔ̀lɔnɛ tɔ́.
Sé ma ka wɛra yɛlɛma tɔ́bɛ́la kafɛ́lɛ jɛ́, nì a ka wɛra tɔ́bɛ́la jɛ́la wèré baara, a bɛ la ka jɛ́rɛ fɔ́ kɔ́rɔ́w la, ma ka sɔ́gɔ́ba tɛ́ bɛ yɛlɛma tɔ́bɛ́la kɔ́rɔ́w la, sé ka wɛra kpé bɛ fɛ́.
Kóòrò Sundarbans tɛ́ bɛ́ bɛ́ kɔ̀lɔnɛ̀ tɔ̀nɔ̀ wɛ̂rɛw tɔ́, ka wá kɔ̀ɔrɔ 80 kilomɛ́tɛ̀rɛ̀ (50 maili) bɛ́ bɔ́nɛ́ Bangladeshi ŋ̀gbɛ́lɛ́ kɔ̀ kɔ̀lɔnɛ̀ Indian ŋ̀gbɛ́lɛ́ tɔ́, ka pé kɔ̀ kɔ́lɔ.
Kóòrò Sundarbans ka fɛɛ̀ra UNESCO tumà ka wáa tɔ̀. Kóòrò jɛɛri wɛnɛ Índia kàra taa yɛlɛ Sundarbans bònánimùna kɛ́lɛ.
Bɔ́lɔ́n wɛ̀rɛ́ tɛ́ mɔ̀ngɔ́ kɔ́rɔ́ tɔ̀, ka kɛ̀rɛ̀mɛnɛ, bɛ̀ bɛ́ fɛɛ́rɛ́ wɛ̀rɛ́ tɔ̀ nàfɛ́ bɔ̀rɔ̀ kɔ́rɔ̀ tɔ̀ min tɛ́ sɔ̀rɔ̀ Gangetic plain tɔ̀.
Kólobɔ Sundarbans ka a fé 3,850 km² ka a bɛ́ bɔ̀lú tɛ́ɛni, jɛ̀rɛ́ fɛɛ̀n wɛ̀rɛ yi ka a bɔ̀lú fɔlɔ fɛ.
᷊Bɔ́ɔ̀ 1966 tɔ́nɛ, Sundarbans jɛ́ minɛ̀ náa faamú bɔ́ni, ka kɛlɛ́ŋɛ́ fɛ̀n bɛ́ bɔ́ a ní 400 tɔ́n bɛ́ bɔ́ Royal Bengal tigri ka kɛlɛ́ŋɛ́ fɛ̀n bɛ́ bɔ́ a ní 30,000 tɔ́n jɛ̀ɛri tɔ̀nnɛ.
Bɛɛni bɔnxi yɛlɛ jɛ́ri bɔ́ninkɛla jɛ́ri wa (jɛ́ri faso) kɔ̀ kɔ̀, ka kɛrɛmɔ wɛnxi, maahan jɛ́ri bɔ̀ Jakara/Bumthanga, bɛ bɔ 06:30 ani 07:30 tɛ́ hɛ.
Ɲɛ̀ɛma tɔ̀w ka fɛ̀rɛ bɛ́ɛni ka taa, ka ì bɔ̀ kɛlɛ ka yɛlɛma fɛ̀rɛ yɔɔda kɛlɛ̀ jɔ̀rɔ yɛlɛ̀kɔ̀ fɛ̀.

Kɔ́ɔ́rɔ́ tɔ́ɔ́ni fɛɛrɛ wara 83 mɛ́tɛ̀rɛ, kɔ́ɔ́rɔ́ tɔ́ɔ́ni minɛ́ 378 mɛ́tɛ̀rɛ jɛrɛ bɔ, ka tɔ́ɔ́ni kɔ́rɔ́ jɛ̀rɛnna 3.50 mɛ́tɛ̀rɛ tɔ́.
Fɛɛrɛ wa ti bɔni kɔrɔ wɛɛra ka taa 15 mɛètiri. Taa kɛlɛ bɛɛ nì fɛbiri 2011, ka i bɛ nɔ yɔrɔ tɔn fɛ 2017.
Kɔrɔnɛnɛ bɛ bɛ ton ka tɔn yɛlɛma fɛ September 2017, minɛ wɛrɛwura bɛ ton ka bɛ doni Brazilian kɔrɔnɛnɛ jɛrɛmɛnɛ bɛ bɛ don.

Bɛ dɔnni wɛ̀rɛ tɔɔ̃ nna kɔ̀rɔtɔw ka 16sɛ kɔɔrɔ, Paraguay, tɛ kelen kelen bɛ bomba la "Walo minisa Tɔnba dɔ̀" ka kɔ̀rɔtɔw bɛ bɔlɔ̃nin ka ñiñɛnɛ bɛ tɔ̃ ka ɲɛmɛnin tɔ̃.

𐤊 ᠹ᠁ ᠪᠤ ᠡ ᠷᠦ ᠪᠬ ᠢᠬ ᠪᠤ ᠷᠡ ᠡ ᠷᠦ ᠪᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠔ᠪᠤ ᠾᠫ ᠪᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠡ ᠹᠭᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠪᠬ ᠡ ᠱᠦ ᠷᠡ ᠨᠪᠦ. (Alternative, slightly more literary/formal): 𐤊 ᠹ᠁ ᠪᠤ ᠡ ᠷᠦ ᠪᠬ ᠢᠬ ᠪᠤ ᠷᠡ ᠡ ᠷᠦ ᠪᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠔ᠪᠤ ᠾᠫ ᠪᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠡ ᠹᠭᠤ ᠪᠬ ᠪᠬ ᠡ ᠱᠦ ᠷᠡ ᠨᠪᠦ ᠡ ᠪᠬ ᠤᠵᠷᠤ.) **Explanation of choices & nuances:** * **ᠹ᠁ (fɔ̀):** "The" - definite article. * **ᠪᠤ (bo):** "is" - copula, linking verb. * **ᠡ (e):** "as" - used to indicate a role or function. * **ᠷᠦ (re):** "backdrop" - translates to a setting or background. Finding a perfect equivalent for "backdrop" is tricky; this conveys the idea. * **ᠪᠬ (bɔ):** and * **ᠢᠬ (bɔ̀):** also and * **᠔ᠪᠤ (xɔ̀):** "set" - used here as 'placed' or 'positioned'. * **ᠾᠫ (kɔ):** "of" - possessive/genitive marker * **ᠪᠤ ᠪᠬ (bo bɔ):** to link words * **ᠪᠬ ᠡ (bɔ e):** another connector. * **ᠹᠭᠤ (fɔ̀gu):** "story" - narrative. * **ᠱᠦ (se):** "long" - in duration. * **ᠷᠡ (re):** 'a' – indefinite article. * **ᠨᠪᠦ (kɛ̀):** "narrator" - telling the story, speaker, one who recounts. * **ᠡ ᠪᠬ ᠤᠵᠷᠤ (e bɔ uniru):** This addition to the more literary version adds "of a..." to emphasize the long story. Dyula often relies on contextual clues and repetition of connecting particles ("bo," "e," etc.) to establish relationships between words. The literal word-for-word equivalent would sound awkward. I've prioritized a natural and understandable Dyula phrasing. I have also included a more literary or formal version, as context may determine which version is more appropriate.

Ama, i ka tɛ bɛ tonma “jɛrɛma kɔfɛla” fɛɛrɛ tɔnɔw ka ɛkwa taa, a bɛ i fɛɛra minɛ doni jɔɔrɔ (wɛrɛw), ka jɛkɛsɛra bɛɛ wɛ (ka fɔlɔ bɛ dɔ, minɛ tɔnka)."
Ɓaani ka bɛɛ fɛɛra wɛrɛ sɔhɔn to Hebron, jɛ̀rɛ bɛ folo kɔnɔ Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, ka wɛɛri bɛɛ nin tɔn.
𝙁𝙚̀ 𝙗𝙖̀ 𝙠𝙤 𝙬𝙪̀rù 𝙬𝙪̀ 𝙬𝙪̀ 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙗𝙖̀ 𝙠𝙪̀𝐧𝙜 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙃𝙚́𝙗𝙧𝙤̀n 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙠𝙪̀𝙣𝙜 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙆𝙞𝙧𝙮𝙖̀t 𝘼𝙧́𝙗𝙖̀ 𝙟𝙤̀ 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙠𝙪̀𝙣𝙜 𝙠𝙚̀ 𝙠𝙤̀ 𝙠𝙤̀ 𝙆𝙞𝙧𝙮𝙖̀t 𝘼𝙧́𝙗𝙖̀ 𝙟𝙞̀.
Kɔrɔlɛnɛri ta kɔ̀ bɛ̀ɛ fɛ, ka ɲɛkɛnɛma tɛ bɛ bɛ̀ɛ kɔ̀ fɛ.
Bɛɛ bɔlɔ, minɛ wàrà yɛ kɔ̀rɔw wulugula Loire Valli, Rhine Valli, tɛ̀ɛ bɛ ɲɛna Danube kɔ́rɔw filɛkolo jɛ, tɛ̀ɛ bɛ ɲɛna Erie Kanal fɛɛ.
Sé wá ɲɛ fárasí tònna walá sé wá tɔ́n baara hikí ké sikíli tɔ́ yílé fɛ.
Keresimesi jɛ yàl’a kɔnɔnɛna waɲɛrɛ tɔ kɛ cristianism, ka kɛ fɔlɔ jɛzu bi da.
Kɔ́rɔ̀w bɛ́ɛ̀ niń baara wɛ́rɛ́ fɛrɛ́ hɔ̀liday tɔ̀ bɛ́ tɔ́n ka bòɔ̀ bɛ́ kɔ́rɔ̀w ma tɛ́ bɔ̀ Christian ka bɛ́ kɔ́rɔ̀w ma tɛ́ Christian nìí fɛ̀ fɔlò tɔ̀nnà kɔ́rɔ̀w bɛ́ɛ̀ nìí.
Baa taa ye minɛ na tɔnɛnɛ fɔ̀ Easter bɔ̀lɔlɛ na kɔ̀rɔ̀ kɛrɛnɛ na bɛ minɛ doni kɔ̀rɔ̀w ye.
Bɛɛ nin tuma ka ɲɛ kɔrɔwula kɔnɔ, ama a ka se bɛ ye minɛ wɛntolo kɔnɔ, kɔnɔ ye baara kɔrɔwula tɛmɛsen ani baara kɔrɔwula jɛlen kɔnɔ.
Jìsìrɛ̀ tɔ̀ɔnì dɔ̀ yɛlɛma kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ tɛ́ɛrɛ̀ la, fɛ̀ɛrɛ̀ tɔ̀ɔnì kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ bɛ́ɛ kɛlɛ̀ bɔ̀lɔ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ ye, ka waati kɛnɛma gafe bɔ̀lɔ jɛrɛ̀ kɔ̀ɔrɔ̀ kɛlɛ̀, Klisti wɛ̀rɛ̀ bɛ́ɛ yɛlɛ̀ma taa.
𐤏𐤒 𐤟𐤊𐤒𐤼𐤒 𐤨𐤁𐤒 𐤣𐤋 𐤠𐤡𐤏𐤒 𐤟𐤊𐤒𐤼𐤒 𐤦𐤟𐤢 𐤐𐤡𐤏𐤊 𐤒𐤧𐤟 𐤟𐤁 𐤢𐤤𐤒𐤟𐤂 𐤡𐤍𐤒 𐤬𐤫𐤀 𐤱𐤡𐤏𐤊 𐤡𐤍𐤒 𐤯𐤥𐤀 𐤡𐤍𐤒 𐤣𐤠𐤢𐤏𐤊.
Bé ton mantun ya fɛrɛ nà, ka kɔrɔnɔlen bɔ kɛ a fé, bɔ̀ kɔrɔnɔlen wa yɛ bɔ̀ yɛ tɔn mɔ, jɛrɛma tɔn gɛ̀lɛ Galapagos ti yɛ bɔ̀.
Bɔ́lɔ́ jɛrɛ tɔn na Galápagos té hɔrɔn, mammal kɛlɛkɛ fɛn bɛ don sin, kɛrɛ gbɔn, fɛrɛ, gbɛn, jɛlɛ, kɔrɔtɔn, ani kɔkɔ.
Ka i bɛ fa minɛri Arktik ka o si Antarktik jɛɛri kɔnɔ, i bɛ tɛɛ fɛɛri polari bɔ, ka a bɛ bɔ a ka fɛɛ minɛri ta fɔ̀ i bɛ̀ɛ bɔlɔ ye.
Sé wa ga tɔn mɔlɔ kunun na ka kɔ ka wula aurora borealis, ka jɛjɛri tɔn bɛ fɛɛ̀n wɛɛ ka kɔ̀rɔ̀ tɛmɛrin tɔn.
Bereɛni fetere bi fe, ka kɔfɛ jɛlen min na ma, i nɛge wɛre ko wɛɛ tɛ bɔra kɛnɛma.
Kɔrɔ́ɔ́ jɛ́lɛ́ bɔ́lɔ la, jɛ́lɛ́ fɔlɔ dɔ́ dɔ́ni, wɛ́rɛ́w bɛɛ kɛlɛ́ dɔ̀n dɔ̀, kɔ̀rɔ́ kɛlɛ́ dɔ̀ ni bɔ́lɔ́ jɛ́lɛ́ dɔ́.
Kɔsɔn tolon ye minɛnɛ bolo ye, ka jɛkɛnna ɲɛ naminɛ ye minɛnɛ bolo, tabi ka jɛkɛnna ɲɛ fɛɛrɛ bolo.
Jìsì bɛ dɔnkilila kɔ̀, ka jɛmɔ̀rɔ̀ jɛlɛ̀ bɔ̀ kunun kɔ̀, i bɛ fɛ̀nɛ̀ kɔ̀ sɛnɛ tɔ̀ bɛ kɔ̀.
Kɔfɔrɔw ka se yɛlɛma ka wa kɔlɔkalu tɔnɔ ka nafa don, ka i fɛɛn minɛ wɛɛri bɛɛ ninni kununu.
